### [205] [Bridge-WA: Predicting Where and How the World Changes for Robotic Action](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02195)
*Yongjie Bai,Hanting Wang,Mingtong Dai,Qijun Zhong,Yang Liu,Liang Lin*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: Bridge-WA提出了一种高效的通用视觉-语言-动作模型框架，通过提炼出轻量级的未来变化先验，有效提升了机器人 manipulation 的表现和泛化能力，尤其在视觉环境变化时表现突出。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的视觉-语言-动作模型虽然依靠大规模先验提升了表现，但在需要精确操作时，常用基于大生成模型或密集未来预测的方式，计算昂贵且关注了与操作关系不大的视觉细节，限制了效率与泛化能力。作者希望通过更高效的方式，专注于与操作相关的场景变化，提升机器人的任务完成度和适应性。

Method: 提出Bridge-WA框架，通过教师-学生范式，将冻结的未来场景变化教师模型提炼为三种紧凑型先验：未来token（代表期望结果）、改变地图（便于识别干预区域）、运动流映射（指示局部过渡方向）。学生模型（WorldBridge）通过多源注意力和时空偏置，将上述先验融入行动变换器中。推理阶段无需教师模型，提升运算效率。

Result: 在VLABench、RoboTwin2.0、LIBERO-Plus、以及真实机器人实验中，Bridge-WA在任务成功率、进展速度和鲁棒性等指标上均优于现有模型，尤其在遇到分布外视觉干扰（如背景、光照、干扰物）时表现提升显著。

Conclusion: Bridge-WA通过聚焦场景真实有效变化，有效压制了无关外观因素，提高了泛化与鲁棒性，无需部署阶段的大规模未来图像生成，提升了机器人 manipulation 的实际应用效果。

Abstract: General-purpose vision-language-action models benefit from large vision-language priors, but effective manipulation also requires anticipating action-relevant scene changes. Existing world-action models often rely on large generative world models or dense future rollouts, which are expensive and spend capacity on visual details weakly coupled to control. We present Bridge-WA, a lightweight world-action framework that distills a frozen future-change teacher into three compact priors: future tokens for intended outcomes, change maps for intervention support, and motion-flow maps for local transition direction. A WorldBridge conditions the action transformer on these priors through multi-source attention memories and spatial-temporal biases, while the teacher model is removed at inference. Across VLABench, RoboTwin2.0, LIBERO-Plus and real-robot evaluations, Bridge-WA improves task success, progress, and robustness, with particularly clear gains under out-of-distribution visual shifts. By focusing action generation on where and how the scene will change, Bridge-WA suppresses nuisance appearance factors such as background, lighting, and distractors, leading to better generalization without deployment-time dense future-image generation. Code and visualizations are available at: https://hcplab-sysu.github.io/BRIDGE-WA .

</details>


### [206] [Actuator Reality Shaping for Zero-Shot Sim-to-Real Robot Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02205)
*Satoshi Yamamori,Koji Ishihara,Kentaro Minamikawa,Kiyoharu Ohomori,Taiyo Yazaki,Norikazu Sugimoto,Jun Morimoto*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本论文提出一种新的Sim-to-Real迁移方法——执行器现实塑形，通过在真实机器人上重塑伺服电机的闭环控制特性，使其与仿真中的理想动力学模型一致，从而实现无须任务级微调的零样本迁移。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有机器人学习中的Sim-to-Real迁移常受限于仿真器和真实机械执行器动力学之间的差距，这导致仿真训练的策略难以直接应用到实际硬件上。传统方法如系统辨识、域随机化或学习型执行器模型虽能缓解这一问题，但都有一定局限性。为根本解决硬件动力学与理想模型不匹配的问题，论文提出了硬件塑形的新思路。

Method: 方法上，每个机械关节配备一个双自由度（前馈-反馈）控制器，将参考响应的塑形与鲁棒稳定性解耦，使物理执行器的输出特性标准化，靠近理想化的二阶参考模型。这样，基于该标准接口训练的强化学习策略无需任何针对目标硬件的学习或微调，即可直接部署到各种实体机器人上。

Result: 该方法在高减速比单关节伺服、7自由度机械臂、轮式-腿式机器人以及类人机器人等多种平台和任务上进行验证，结果显示相比标准伺服和主流基线，现实塑形显著降低了Sim-to-Real误差，提高了任务零样本迁移性能。

Conclusion: 执行器现实塑形为机器人学习提供了一个可复用的标准化接口，大幅简化了不同硬件平台间的策略迁移流程，有望成为面向多样机器人系统的有效Sim-to-Real迁移方案。

Abstract: Sim-to-real transfer in robot learning is often limited by discrepancies between the ideal actuator dynamics assumed during policy training and the nonlinear, hardware-dependent behavior of physical motors. While conventional approaches attempt to bridge this gap by increasing simulator fidelity through system identification, domain randomization, or learned actuator models, we introduce an alternative paradigm: actuator reality shaping. Instead of modifying the simulator to match the real world, our method shapes the closed-loop behavior of physical actuators to match the idealized second-order reference dynamics used in simulation. By equipping each joint with a two-degree-of-freedom feedforward--feedback controller, we decouple reference-response shaping from robust stabilization, thereby providing a standardized actuator interface for reinforcement learning policies. As a result, policies trained only with the prescribed reference model can be deployed zero-shot on real hardware without task-level fine-tuning or learned actuator models. We validate the approach on a single-joint high-gear-ratio servo under external loads and a 7-DOF robotic arm reaching task, where actuator reality shaping substantially reduces sim-to-real tracking error and improves zero-shot task performance compared with standard servo-control and representative real-to-sim-to-real baselines. We further demonstrate zero-shot transfer on a wheeled-legged robot driving over a slope and a humanoid robot walking, suggesting that actuator reality shaping can serve as a reusable interface for robot learning across diverse hardware platforms.

</details>


### [207] [CoFL-S: Spatially Queryable Sector Flow Fields for Local Language-Conditioned Navigation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02222)
*Haokun Liu,Zhaoqi Ma,Yicheng Chen,Wentao Zhang,Masaki Kitagawa,Zicen Xiong,Jinjie Li,Moju Zhao*

Method: 提出了CoFL-S框架，在机器人本地视野下预测受语言条件影响的流场，从而生成连续导航轨迹。为训练此底层表示，将导航任务转换为逐帧的局部监督信号，细致对齐子指令、动作、轨迹以及流场目标。评测方法设计了连续时间的Habitat基准，解耦动作执行与任务分解，用统一控制器公平比较不同方法，从而更好地反映框架效果。

Abstract: Vision-Language Navigation has increasingly emphasized high-level instruction reasoning, memory, global map construction, and instruction decomposition, while the low-level action representation remains comparatively underexplored. To train this low-level representation, we convert each VLN-CE episode, originally a whole-episode instruction paired with an action sequence, into frame-level local supervision with aligned sub-instructions and matched action, trajectory, and dense flow-field targets. For evaluation, we introduce a continuous-time Habitat benchmark that isolates low-level action interfaces from instruction decomposition and executes all methods through a shared velocity-command controller, enabling decomposition-independent closed-loop comparison across different planner frequencies rather than fixed discrete forward-and-turn transitions in VLN-CE. Under matched encoders and training settings, CoFL-S consistently outperforms action-token and action-chunk baselines across planner frequencies in the continuous-time Habitat benchmark, and zero-shot real-world closed-loop deployment further shows its advantage over both baselines beyond simulation.

Across 72 simulated landing scenarios spanning diverse terrains, NEUROSYMLAND achieves 61 successful assessments, outperforming four competitive baselines (37-57 successes). To evaluate deployability, we further conduct 100 hardware-in-the-loop trials with randomized initial poses, profiling end-to-end latency, stage-wise execution time, and system-level metrics including CPU/GPU utilization, memory footprint, and power consumption. Results demonstrate improved robustness and interpretability with bounded edge-resource usage. Profiling shows that symbolic reasoning contributes only a small fraction of end-to-end latency, while the main computational cost arises from perception and PSSG construction. ### [210] [The Moving Eye: Enhancing VLA Spatial Generalization via Hybrid Dynamic Data Collection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02322)
*Jincheng Tang,Yilong Zhu,Zhengyuan Xie,Jiang-Jiang Liu,Jiaxing Zhang*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 该论文针对VLA（视觉-语言-动作）模型空间泛化能力差的问题，提出将移动相机与多样静态视角结合的数据采集策略，显著提升模型对新视角和物体配置的泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: VLA模型在复杂机器人操作任务中表现优异，但在空间泛化（即对未见摄像机视角和物体布局的适应）上仍表现脆弱。此前主要做法是增加摄像机视角数量，但仍未有效消除“捷径学习”问题——模型容易依赖无关的相关性（如固定相对位置）而非真正空间关系。本研究希望找出一种从源头（数据采集）解决泛化瓶颈的策略。

Method: 采用双机械臂系统，其中一臂操控，另一臂作为可移动环境摄像头。实验系统性地比较了三种数据分布方式：固定视角、多点固定视角、连续移动视角。进一步提出混合策略：将可持续移动的摄像头与多个静态视角结合进行数据采集。

Result: 实验结果表明，单纯增加静态视角不足以提升空间泛化，而混合策略（连续移动+多静态视角）能显著减少虚假相关性，提升模型对新视角和新物体布局的适应能力。多种VLA架构（ACT、Diffusion、Pi0、Gr00t等）均受益明显。

Conclusion: VLA模型普遍存在空间泛化弱、易捷径学习的问题，简单扩充数据无效。混合移动和静态视角采集的数据策略能系统性解决上述问题，对多种体系结构均有提升，拓展了VLA模型的泛化能力和实际应用前景。

Abstract: Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models have shown remarkable promise in generalized robotic manipulation. However, their spatial generalization remains fragile. We argue that simply increasing the number of viewpoints is insufficient. Models often fall into the trap of Shortcut Learning, latching onto spurious correlations (e.g., fixed relative poses between objects or between the camera and robot base) rather than learning true spatial relationships. In this work, we propose a data-centric solution to enhance VLA spatial generalization. We utilize a dual-arm setup where one arm performs manipulation while the other serves as a mobile environmental camera. We systematically evaluate three data distribution patterns: Fixed, Multi-Fixed, and Moving Views. Our findings reveal that a hybrid strategy, combining continuous camera motion with diverse static viewpoints, yields the best performance by substantially reducing spurious correlations while maintaining training stability. Our experiments demonstrate that this strategy mitigates spurious correlations, enabling VLAs to generalize to unseen camera poses and object configurations where simply adding more static viewpoints fails. Crucially, we reveal that the susceptibility to shortcut learning and the struggle with spatial generalization are universal characteristics shared across diverse architectures. Consequently, all evaluated models (ACT, Diffusion, and VLA models including Pi0 and Gr00t) benefit significantly from our mixed data strategy.

### [212] [ACID: Action Consistency via Inverse Dynamics for Planning with World Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02403)
*Gawon Seo,Dongwon Kim,Suha Kwak*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 提出一种新的决策时规划框架ACID，通过引入循环动作一致性提升规划效果，在多种控制任务和世界模型上都能提高效率和保持甚至提升准确率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于动作条件世界模型的决策时规划方法仅根据最终状态与目标的接近程度评判规划轨迹，而未关注中间状态的可实现性，导致预测轨迹与真实环境演化偏离。为解决该缺陷，需增强轨迹中各步动作与逆动力学模型的一致性。

Method: ACID 框架在规划过程中引入循环动作一致性机制：利用逆动力学模型对预测的每一步转移倒推出动作，并要求其与原始输入动作相符。每一步的一致性损失被自适应、尺度无关地加入到总规划代价中，从而避免不切实际的规划结果。

Result: ACID在四种动作条件世界模型和六类任务（包括刚体与可变形体操作、关节控制和视觉导航）上进行了实验，无论任务和模型类型，均稳步提升了规划效果，且在减少大量计算量的前提下达到或超过基线方法的表现。

Conclusion: 引入循环动作一致性的ACID规划框架，在确保轨迹可实现性的同时提升决策时规划性能，兼具高效性和准确性，适用于多种复杂的控制和操作任务。

Abstract: Decision-time planning with action-conditioned world models has become a popular paradigm for embodied control. However, the standard planning cost judges a candidate solely by how close its predicted terminal state lies to the goal, leaving the realizability of the intermediate transitions unchecked -- a predicted trajectory can look convincing while the environment rollout drifts away from it. In this paper, we propose ACID, a decision-time planning framework that introduces cycle action consistency: the action inferred backward from a predicted transition by an inverse dynamics model should recover the one that was conditioned on. We fold this per-step residual into the planning cost via a scale-invariant adaptive weight. Across four action-conditioned world models and six tasks spanning rigid and deformable manipulation, articulated control, and visual navigation, ACID consistently improves planning and matches the baseline's accuracy with substantially less planning compute.

</details>


### [213] [LIME: Learning Intent-aware Camera Motion from Egocentric Video](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02417)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的机器人研究主要关注语言驱动的导航或操作动作，较少关注基于语言的相机运动。相机运动对机器人根据意图感知环境尤为关键，如揭示遮挡、检查物体等。

Method: 作者将语言条件下的相机运动任务形式化，即输入当前视觉观测与自然语言意图，预测下一帧相机的相对位姿。论文通过从第一视角视频中挖掘多意图相机位姿监督，并提出LIME模型，结合自回归观测增益输出与连续流匹配位姿预测头，可同时预测想要观察的内容及对应可能的多目标位姿。

Abstract: Autonomous robots often need to move their camera before they can act: to inspect an object, reveal an occluded region, or obtain a view that responds to a user's intent. While vision-language navigation translates instructions to base motion and vision-language-action policies map instructions to manipulation actions, language-conditioned camera motion remains comparatively underexplored as a first-class action. We formulate language-conditioned camera motion generation: given a current RGB observation and a free-form natural-language intent, predict a relative target camera pose for the next observation. This task is inherently non-trivial: viewpoint changes are driven by latent perceptual intentions, and a valid motion may operate at different semantic granularity, from entering a room to looking around a corner, inspecting a visible object, or revealing an occluded detail. To model this structure, we mine multi-intention camera-motion supervision from egocentric video, pairing plausible intents and observation-gain descriptions with relative SE(3) target poses. We propose LIME, a vision-language camera-motion generator that combines an auto-regressive observation-gain output with a continuous flow-matching pose head. This design lets the model jointly predict what the next view should reveal while representing multi-hypothesis target views. Across experiments and downstream robotic tasks, we show that LIME can learn to actively choose camera poses from passive human video, turning ordinary egocentric recordings into supervision for intent-aware active perception.

### [214] [WorldSample: Closed-loop Real-robot RL with World Modelling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02431)
*Yuquan Xue,Le Xu,Zeyi Liu,Zhenyu Wu,Zhengyi Gu,Xinyang Song,Bofang Jia,Ziwei Wang*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 该论文提出WorldSample框架，通过结合真实机器人执行与高保真世界模型生成的虚拟转移数据，有效提升了强化学习在机器人任务上的效率和表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统模仿学习因示范覆盖有限而受限，强化学习虽可突破但真实机器人上交互成本极高。作者致力于解决如何在降低物理交互次数的前提下，提升机器人强化学习表现。

Method: WorldSample利用真实机器人的执行数据训练高保真的世界模型，用以生成合成转移数据。创新性地提出Policy-Paced Learning (PPL)，通过动态样本选择和调度，平衡数据增强与价值高估风险，减小虚假数据噪声。

Result: 在机器人精细操作任务上，WorldSample相较基线算法将策略成功率提高28%，训练步数减少59%。世界模型视觉保真度（PSNR、SSIM）提升显著。

Conclusion: WorldSample高效结合物理与虚拟数据，显著提升机器人强化学习效率和世界模型表现，为真实机器人强化学习提供了可行且高效的途径。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning (RL) can overcome the demonstration-coverage limitation of imitation learning (IL) by allowing robots to improve through trial-and-error interaction beyond the states observed in demonstrations. However, deploying RL on real robots remains constrained by high interaction costs, since each physical rollout is costly and reflects only one realized action-outcome path. To address this challenge, we propose WorldSample, a physically grounded data augmentation framework for real-robot RL that closes a real-synthetic loop between physical rollouts, world-model generation, and policy improvement. Grounded on real rollouts, WorldSample generates high-fidelity synthetic transitions through a post-trained world model, which greatly lowers the visual hallucination. Specifically, rather than simply using these transitions as real-world experience, WorldSample introduces Policy-Paced Learning (PPL) to regulate the training process through sample selection and scheduling, balancing useful augmentation against value overestimation and mitigating the hallucination-induced noise. Experiments on robot manipulation tasks involving contact-rich and precise tasks show that WorldSample improves policy success rate by 28% while reducing training steps by 59% compared with baselines. Furthermore, WorldSample improves world model visual fidelity by 19.4dB in PSNR and 0.47 in SSIM over demonstration-only post-training, validating the effectiveness of the real-synthetic loop for both policy and world model performance.

### [215] [Learning to Move Before Learning to Do: Task-Agnostic pretraining for VLAs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02466)
*Junhao Shi,Siyin Wang,Xiaopeng Yu,Li Ji,Jingjing Gong,Xipeng Qiu*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种两阶段VLA模型预训练框架TAP（Task-Agnostic Pretraining），用廉价无标签数据自监督学习运动能力，再用极少专家数据进行语言对齐，在大幅减少标注数据下取得与传统方法相近或更好的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: VLA模型依赖专家数据（三元组：观测、指令、动作），收集成本高，限制模型扩展。作者发现运动能力与任务语义对齐其实是两个不同的目标，后者才真正需要语言数据，因此提出用拆解学习目标降低成本。

Method: 提出Task-Agnostic Pretraining（TAP）方法，分两阶段：第一阶段用无标签数据和自监督Inverse Dynamics学习物理运动先验；第二阶段用极少量专家数据，将运动先验与语言对齐，实现语义理解。

Result: TAP在SIMPLER基准上使用远少于现有方法的专家数据就取得相当或更优成绩，比标准行为克隆法高10%；在实际机器人平台上，即使摄像头出现杂散扰动，TAP成功率仍达25%，而基于海量互联网数据的基线方法降为0%。

Conclusion: TAP能有效分离运动与语义的学习目标，大幅节省专家标注数据的需求，生成更稳健、可迁移的物理表示，为具身智能AI预训练提供了可扩展的解决方案。

Abstract: Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models are fundamentally bottlenecked by the scarcity of expert demonstrations -- triplets of observations, instructions, and actions that are costly to collect at scale. We argue that this bottleneck stems from conflating two distinct learning objectives: acquiring physical competence (how to move) and acquiring semantic alignment (what to do). Crucially, only the latter requires language supervision. Building on this Decomposition Hypothesis, we propose Task-Agnostic Pretraining (TAP), a two-stage framework that first learns transferable motor priors from cheap, unlabeled interaction data -- including discarded off-task trajectories and autonomous robot play -- via a self-supervised Inverse Dynamics objective. A lightweight second stage then grounds these priors in language using minimal expert data. On the SIMPLER benchmark, TAP matches models trained on over 1M expert trajectories while using orders of magnitude less labeled data, yielding a 10% absolute gain over standard behavior cloning. On a real-world WidowX platform, TAP retains 25% success under camera perturbations where internet-scale baselines collapse to 0%, demonstrating that task-agnostic pretraining produces robust, transferable physical representations and offers a scalable path forward for Embodied AI.

</details>


### [216] [Learning Agile Intruder Interception using Differentiable Quadrotor Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02472)
*Michael Anoruo,Xiaoyu Tian,Abhishek Rathod,Timothy Naudet,Thomas Canchola,Eric Sturzinger,Kshitij Goel,Wennie Tabib*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于3D方向向量和拦截者状态的无人机拦截策略学习方法，通过可微分的四旋翼动力学和解析策略梯度方法，实现了高达10m/s的敏捷拦截，性能优于现有基线方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有深度强化学习拦截方法通常假设可获得入侵者的相对位置或距离信息，但实际应用中使用被动单目摄像头时，无法直接获取这些信息，因此需寻找新方法。

Method: 利用3D方向单位向量和拦截者自身状态作为输入，采用可微分的四旋翼动力学和解析策略梯度算法进行拦截策略学习，无需依赖精确的位置信息。

Result: 所提出方法在达到高达10m/s的速度下，拦截性能较基于简化点质量动力学的基线方法平均提升约30%。

Conclusion: 通过结合可微分动力学模型与解析策略梯度，可以在有限传感信息条件下实现更高效、更敏捷的无人机拦截控制，为实际系统部署提供了改进途径。

Abstract: This paper presents a methodology for learning a control policy to intercept an intruder using the 3D direction unit vector to the intruder and the interceptor state. Prior deep reinforcement learning approaches assume either relative position or distance to the intruder is available, but this information is not readily accessible in real-world applications that employ passive, monocular camera sensors. Instead, we propose a solution that leverages an analytical policy gradient method using differentiable quadrotor dynamics to learn agile interception at speeds up to 10 m/s. The proposed approach outperforms baseline methods that utilize simplified point mass dynamics by an average of 30%.

</details>


### [217] [QuadRocket: An Aerial Robotic Testbed for Adaptive Thrust-Vector Control of Rocket-Like Vehicles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02474)
*Pedro Santos,Joel Reis,Paulo Oliveira,Carlos Silvestre*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了QuadRocket，这是一种基于四旋翼的火箭原型，用于低成本、低风险验证推进矢量控制策略，并通过仿真和实验证实了其有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有推进矢量控制系统的研发和测试成本高、风险大，因此需要一种便于研究、低成本、安全的实验平台。

Method: 作者设计了一种将气缸体通过万向节安装在四旋翼上的倒立摆系统，并进行了系统建模、简化和分解。创新地采用了二球面上的简化姿态表示，开发了自适应反步控制器并结合动态面姿态控制，有效实现矢量跟踪和干扰抑制。

Result: 通过仿真和室内实验验证，系统能够实现高精度轨迹跟踪和干扰补偿，表现出良好的控制效果和平台适用性。

Conclusion: QuadRocket能作为推进矢量控制系统的有效实验平台，为火箭类系统相关控制策略的研发和测试提供了低风险、低成本的实现途径。

Abstract: This paper presents QuadRocket, a quadrotor-based rocket prototype that provides a low-cost, low-risk platform for validating advanced thrust-vector control strategies for launch vehicle-type systems. The prototype consists of a cylindrical main body mounted on top of a quadrotor through a universal joint, forming a flying inverted pendulum with non-negligible inertia. For control design, the coupled system is modeled as a single axisymmetric rigid body actuated by a vectored force applied along its longitudinal axis. A reduced-attitude representation on the two sphere is adopted to explicitly exploit the vehicle's axial symmetry and to decouple yaw from the thrust-vector direction. On this model, we derive an adaptive backstepping controller that achieves almost global trajectory tracking in the presence of unknown constant disturbances, while a control-point transformation mitigates non minimum-phase behavior. The quadrotor is then treated as a thrust vector actuator, and a dynamic-surface-based attitude controller is designed to track the desired thrust-vector, accounting for actuation dynamics and avoiding explicit differentiation of virtual control signals. The complete architecture is evaluated in simulation and validated experimentally in an indoor motion-capture arena. Results demonstrate accurate trajectory tracking, effective disturbance compensation, and confirm the suitability of the QuadRocket as a versatile testbed for thrust-vector-controlled robotic vehicles.

</details>


### [218] [Controllable Sim Agents with Behavior Latents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02496)
*Juanwu Lu,Junyu Zhu,Ziran Wang*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种可控的神经变分智能体（CNeVA），能够在交通仿真中实现基于各项物理指标（如速度、安全性等）的实时可控，同时模拟现实中的驾驶行为。通过结构性的改进，实现了更好的仿真真实性和可控性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前的交通仿真智能体往往缺乏对特定行为通道（如速度、加速度、安全性等）的精细可控性，这限制了仿真用于自动驾驶测试和极端场景复现的能力。工程师亟需一种既真实又能按需操纵的模拟体，以支持更有针对性的系统测试和分析。

Method: 作者提出CNeVA框架：针对每个智能体，通过“每通道贴现回报”推断其高斯行为潜变量，并用封闭式共轭变分更新算法优化；轨迹生成器基于混合通道遮罩课程训练，实现分类器自由引导。为缓解奖励信号稀缺问题，提出“软有效性门”机制，通过指数衰减而非硬阈值保持梯度信息。

Result: 在Waymo Open Motion Dataset上，CNeVA在仿真真实性基准测试中取得了有竞争力的表现，并独特实现了针对各行为通道的可控性（高排名模仿模型普遍缺乏）。速度、加速度等可控指标呈单调响应，摒弃了奖励劫持；引入软有效性后，安全性可控性也显著增强，实现了基于地图的合规可控性。

Conclusion: CNeVA能够在保持高逼真度的同时，实现对关键行为指标的灵活操控，满足实际交通仿真的需求。实验还表明，解析“可控性指标”时需与物理合理性约束配套考虑，以避免奖励劫持等异常现象。

Abstract: Realistic traffic simulation requires agents that imitate logged behavior and can also be steered along interpretable axes. Such controllability enables engineers to isolate variables, reproduce specific edge cases, and test autonomous systems without real-world risk. We introduce Controllable Neural Variational Agents (CNeVA), a controllable simulated-agent framework that learns to infer a per-agent Gaussian behavior latent from per-channel discounted returns via a closed-form conjugate variational update, conditioning a rectified-flow trajectory generator trained on a mixed channel-mask curriculum for classifier-free guidance. To tackle scarcity in reward signals, we propose soft eligibility gates that replace hard binary thresholds with smooth exponential decay, preserving the gradient signal for near-threshold agents. On the Waymo Open Motion Dataset, CNeVA attains competitive realism on the benchmark while exposing per-channel controllability that the higher-ranked imitation models lack. Speed- and acceleration-based steering produces monotone responses without stall-induced reward hacking. Safety controllability is monotone and substantial with the introduction of soft eligibility. We manage to achieve steerable map compliance under a context-residual return measure. Furthermore, our experiment demonstrates that steering metrics must be read alongside physical-plausibility guardrails to avoid reward-hacking confounds.

</details>


### [219] [Embodied.cpp: A Portable Inference Runtime of Embodied AI Models on Heterogeneous Robots](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02501)
*Ling Xu,Chuyu Han,Borui Li,Hao Wu,Shiqi Jiang,Ting Cao,Chuanyou Li,Sheng Zhong,Shuai Wang*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 提出了Embodied.cpp——一种用于体感AI模型的通用C++推理运行时，实现了在异构硬件设备上的高效、低延迟、可扩展推理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前体感AI模型（如视觉-语言-动作模型和世界-动作模型）在实际部署中面临着平台碎片化、推理运行时不支持闭环多速率执行、难以适配异构硬件等难题，影响了模型的推广与高效应用。

Method: 设计并实现了Embodied.cpp，通过体系结构分析，将体感AI模型的执行流程抽象为输入适配器、序列生成器、主干执行、头部插件、部署适配器五层，支持多速率、高融合、低延迟推理和可扩展的操作/接口，并统一了不同设备、机器人与仿真器的后端抽象。

Result: 采用Embodied.cpp在两类VLA模型（HY-VLA和pi0.5）和WAM基准（LingBot-VA Transformer block）上测试，VLA模型分别达到了100%和91%的闭环任务成功率，WAM模型内存消耗减少了近4倍，精度保持高水平。

Conclusion: Embodied.cpp极大提升了体感AI模型在异构设备上的部署效率，并兼顾了多模型架构下的高推理精度和系统可扩展性。

Abstract: Embodied AI models now span vision-language-action (VLA) models and world-action models (WAMs), but practical deployment remains fragmented across model-specific Python stacks, backend assumptions, and robot-side glue code, especially on heterogeneous edge devices. Existing inference runtimes are designed mainly for request-response serving and therefore do not satisfy the runtime contract of embodied deployment: multi-rate execution inside closed-loop control, latency-first batch-1 inference on heterogeneous hardware, and extensible embodied interfaces beyond fixed token I/O. We present Embodied.cpp, a portable C++ inference runtime for embodied models. Based on an architectural analysis of representative VLA models and WAMs, Embodied.cpp captures a shared execution path and organizes it into five layers: input adapters, sequence builders, backbone execution, head plugins, and deployment adapters. The runtime provides modular multi-rate execution, latency-first fused inference, and extensible operator and I/O support, enabling deployment across heterogeneous devices, robots, and simulators through one backend abstraction. We evaluate Embodied.cpp on two VLA models, HY-VLA and pi0.5, and on a preliminary WAM benchmark using a LingBot-VA Transformer block. The VLA deployments achieve successful closed-loop execution with 100.0% and 91.0% task success rates, respectively. The WAM benchmark reduces block memory from 312.2 MiB to 88.1 MiB. These results show that Embodied.cpp improves deployment efficiency while preserving high accuracy across diverse embodied model architectures.

</details>


### [220] [VT-WAM: Visual-Tactile World Action Model for Contact-Rich Manipulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02503)
*Shuai Tian,Yupeng Zheng,Yuhang Zheng,Songen Gu,Yujie Zang,Yuxing Qin,Weize Li,Haoran Li,Wenchao Ding,Dongbin Zhao*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了VT-WAM，一个结合视觉和触觉的动作生成模型，用于提升复杂接触操作的表现。相比已有方法，其在多项任务中表现优异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在接触丰富的操作任务中，部分关键感知信息（如触觉变形、压力、打滑和摩擦）难以通过视觉捕捉且具有时间稀疏性，现有方法很少对触觉动态进行建模，导致反应不及时或不准确。

Method: 提出VT-WAM模型，融合视觉预测、触觉变形预测与动作预测，并引入非对称变换器注意力机制（MoT）及基于接触门控的多模态注意引导（AVTAG），提升模型对关键触觉信息的关注。

Result: 在六项真实世界的接触丰富操作任务中，VT-WAM平均成功率达71.67%，分别比Fast-WAM和OmniVTLA高26.67%和35.84%。消融实验验证了触觉动态建模和接触阶段触觉注意力引导的重要性。

Conclusion: 建模触觉变形动态并在动作生成中引导触觉注意力，对提升接触操作任务的表现至关重要，VT-WAM显著优于现有方法。

Abstract: Contact-rich manipulation requires policies to react to local deformation, pressure, slip, and friction, yet these cues are temporally sparse and often invisible in visual observations. Existing visual-tactile policies usually feed tactile observations directly into action prediction, but rarely model tactile deformation dynamics during action generation. In this paper, we introduce VT-WAM, a Visual-Tactile World Action Model that jointly learns future visual prediction, tactile deformation prediction, and action prediction within a unified flow matching framework. In particular, VT-WAM introduces (1) Asymmetric Mixture-of-Transformers (MoT) attention to bridge a first-frame visual anchor with temporal tactile dynamics, and (2) contact-gated Action-Visual-Tactile Attention Guidance (AVTAG) to encourage action queries to rely on tactile evidence during contact phases. Across six real-world contact-rich manipulation tasks, VT-WAM achieves a 71.67% average success rate, outperforming Fast-WAM by 26.67% and OmniVTLA by 35.84%. Ablations demonstrate that modeling tactile deformation dynamics and guiding contact-phase tactile attention are both important for contact-rich tasks. Project website: https://vt-wam.github.io/.

</details>
